  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \

          wget \
          curl \
          git \

          libtiff-dev \
          libopenslide-dev \
          gdal-bin \
          libgdal-dev \
          python3-pip \
          python3-dev \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-wheel \
          htop \
          tmux \
          unzip \
          locales \
          pkg-config \
          software-properties-common \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Setup locale
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  # Install Miniconda (23.10.0-1, x86_64) and Python 3.10
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py310_23.10.0-1-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Update conda and create base environment with Python 3.10
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda && \
      conda install -y python=3.10 && \
      conda clean -afy
  # Add conda to PATH
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Set working directory

NEXT:
  current progress
  - Dockerfile is configured for CPU-only, amd64/x86_64, with no CUDA or GPU-specific dependencies.
  - System packages for CPU, scientific, and image processing libraries are installed (libopenslide, gdal, etc.).
  - Miniconda (Python 3.10) is installed.
  - PyTorch CPU-only versions are installed.
  - requirements.txt is copied and installed.
  - Jupyter, development, and test tools are installed.
  - Docker build fails at `pip install openslide-python gdal` step due to a build error for 'gdal'.
  - Dockerfile starts with `FROM --platform=linux/amd64`, which triggers a warning (platform specifier should not be in the Dockerfile for best practice).
  next step
  1. Remove or comment out the `RUN pip install openslide-python gdal` line and rebuild.  
     - `gdal` and `openslide` Python bindings are often incompatible with pip wheels in many environments, especially when system libraries are already installed.  
     - Instead, rely on system installations (`libgdal-dev`, `gdal-bin`, `libopenslide-dev`) and, if Python bindings are needed, install them via conda or ensure required wheels are present in requirements.txt.
  2. If Python bindings are required, add `RUN conda install -y -c conda-forge gdal openslide-python && conda clean -afy` before the pip install steps.
  3. Remove `--platform=linux/amd64` from the `FROM` line in the Dockerfile; specify the platform only at docker build time with `docker build --platform=linux/amd64 ...`.
  4. Rebuild the Docker image and verify build success.

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \

      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda \

      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          curl \
          git \
          ca-certificates \
          build-essential \
          gcc \
          g++ \
          binutils \
          make \

          libpng-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libtiff-dev \
          libopenslide-dev \

          libgdal-dev \

          python3-dev \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-wheel \
          htop \
          tmux \
          unzip \
          locales \
          pkg-config \
          software-properties-common \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py310_23.10.0-1-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda && \
      conda install -y python=3.10 && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  WORKDIR /CellViT-plus-plus
  COPY requirements.txt ./requirements.txt
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip && \
      if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then pip install -r requirements.txt; fi
  RUN pip install torch==2.2.1 torchvision==0.17.1 torchaudio==2.2.1
  RUN pip install jupyter notebook jupyterlab \
      pytest pre-commit black flake8 ruff pip-tools
  RUN pip install openslide-python gdal
  RUN if [ -f setup.py ]; then pip install -e .; fi
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH \
      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda \
      PYTHONNOUSERSITE=1
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          curl \
          git \
          ca-certificates \
          build-essential \
          gcc \
          g++ \
          binutils \
          make \
          libvips-dev \
          libjpeg-dev \
          libpng-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libtiff-dev \
          libopenslide-dev \

          libgdal-dev \

          python3-setuptools \
          python3-wheel \
          htop \
          tmux \
          unzip \
          locales \
          pkg-config \
          software-properties-common \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8 && update-locale LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py310_23.10.0-1-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda && \
      conda install -y python=3.10 && \
      conda clean -afy
  RUN conda install -y -c conda-forge gdal openslide-python && conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  WORKDIR /CellViT-plus-plus
  COPY requirements.txt ./requirements.txt
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip && \
      if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then pip install -r requirements.txt; fi
  RUN pip install torch==2.2.1 torchvision==0.17.1 torchaudio==2.2.1
  RUN pip install jupyter notebook jupyterlab \
      pytest pre-commit black flake8 ruff pip-tools
  RUN if [ -f setup.py ]; then pip install -e .; fi
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
